     503           1 :   const TimingParams& timing = aAnimation->GetEffect()->SpecifiedTiming();
     504             : 
     505             :   // If we are starting a new transition that replaces an existing transition
     506             :   // running on the compositor, it is possible that the animation on the
     507             :   // compositor will have advanced ahead of the main thread. If we use as
     508             :   // the starting point of the new transition, the current value of the
     509             :   // replaced transition as calculated on the main thread using the refresh
     510             :   // driver time, the new transition will jump when it starts. Instead, we
     511             :   // re-calculate the starting point of the new transition by applying the
     512             :   // current TimeStamp to the parameters of the replaced transition.
     513             :   //
     514             :   // We need to do this here, rather than when we generate the new transition,
     515             :   // since after generating the new transition other requestAnimationFrame
     516             :   // callbacks may run that introduce further lag between the main thread and
     517             :   // the compositor.
